But because of the nature of these documents it is critical for a corporation to enable its employees to consume the documents also on corporate enabled mobile devices like Smartphones or Tablets to be able to be informed in time when travelling.\r\n\r\n\r\nThe RMS Viewer App registers itself to the file types available for RMS and when rights management protection is detected, the mobile app sends the protected document to a RMS Rendering server hosted in the corporate network. When you stop the function clicking on \"Stop follow me\" , the route will be stored in the device. This way, if you go from point A to point B, you can record the route.\r\n\r\n3) Follow me and don't draw route on the map. In the menu you must click on \"Start follow me / Stop follow me\".
